        function reveal() {
                var reveals = document.querySelectorAll("#imark_newsletter, .not-a-thing");
                let bodyElement = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
                for (var i = 0; i < reveals.length; i++) {
                        var windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
                        var elementTop = reveals[i].getBoundingClientRect().top;
                        var elementVisible = reveals[i].offsetHeight - 50;
                        var divID = reveals[i].getAttribute('id');
                        if (elementTop < windowHeight - elementVisible) {
                                if(! reveals[i].classList.contains('animate_triggred') ){
                                        bodyElement.classList.add("promote-active");
                                        reveals[i].classList.add("active-promote");
                                }
                        }
                        if ( elementTop < 200 ) {
                                reveals[i].classList.remove("active-promote");
                                reveals[i].classList.add("animate_triggred");
                                bodyElement.classList.remove("promote-active");
                        }
                }
        }

        var animItem = [];
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
                window.addEventListener("scroll", reveal);
                var cookies_disable = '';
                if( getCookie('promote_disable') == 'wait' && cookies_disable == '' ) {
                        var reveals = document.querySelectorAll(".imark_newsletter");
                        reveals[0].classList.add("animate_triggred");
                }
                // reveal();
        });
        
        window.addEventListener("click", function(){
                let bodyElement = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
                var reveals = document.querySelectorAll("#imark_newsletter, .not-a-thing");
                bodyElement.classList.remove("promote-active");
                for (var i = 0; i < reveals.length; i++) {
                        if( reveals[i].classList.contains('active-promote') ){
                                reveals[i].classList.add("animate_triggred");
                        }
                        if( reveals[i].classList.contains('imark_newsletter') ) { 
                                setCookie( 'promote_disable', 'wait', 1 );
                        }
                }
        });

        function setCookie( cname, cvalue, exdays ) {
                const d = new Date();
                d.setTime( d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                let expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/;SameSite=Lax" + (location.protocol === 'https:' ? ';Secure' : '');
        }

        function getCookie(cname) {
                let name = cname + "=";
                let ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                for(let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                        let c = ca[i];
                        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                                c = c.substring(1);
                        }
                        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                                return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                        }
                }
                return "";
        }

	<header class="page-header">
		<h1 class="entry-title page-title">Essential Advice for Dog Owners, from Licensed Veterinarians and Certified Trainers</h1>	</header>
		<div class="entry-content clearfix">
		
<p>If you are anything like us, you love your dog and have built an incredible bond with your favorite companion. We are here to help: we are a <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/meet-our-team/">team of veterinarians and dog trainers</a> who provide expert advice to keep your dog healthy &amp; happy.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="1000" height="500" src="https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/team_homep.jpg" alt="veterinarian and dog trainer at work" class="wp-image-10389" srcset="https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/team_homep.jpg 1000w, https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/team_homep-300x150.jpg 300w, https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/team_homep-768x384.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px" /></figure>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img decoding="async" width="1000" height="100" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;1000&#039;%20height=&#039;100&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%201000%20100&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="as seen on logos" class="wp-image-9572 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/As-seen-on-Dec3.jpg" data-srcset="https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/As-seen-on-Dec3.jpg 1000w, https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/As-seen-on-Dec3-300x30.jpg 300w, https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/As-seen-on-Dec3-768x77.jpg 768w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px" /></figure>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Our Veterinarians In The News:</h3>



<p>Media outlets often turn to &#8216;Senior Tail Waggers&#8217; for expert insights. Our veterinarians have been featured in over 40 top publications, including <em>Dogster Magazine</em> and <em>The Wall Street Journal</em>. See examples below:</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Our Mission: Rescuing Dogs &amp; Elevating the Well-Being of All Pets</h2>



<p>It’s our mission to 1) save many thousands of rescue pets by giving them greater comfort and care within a “fur-ever” home, and, 2) elevate the health and well-being of pets through constantly expanding educational resources that we freely provide to pet owners. Learn how we achieve this <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/our-mission/">mission</a>.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Featured Health &amp; Wellness Articles from Our Veterinarians</h2>



<p>Our <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/meet-our-team/">veterinarians</a> have over 100 years of combined experience.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Our Dog Trainers Explain Common Dog Behaviors</h2>



<p>We are proud to present a collection of thoroughly reviewed articles written with insights from our certified dog trainers, including <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/team/mindy-waite-phd/">Mindy Waite (Ph.D., CAAB, CPDT-KA)</a> who holds a Ph.D. in animal behavior, and <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/team/julie-burgess/">Julie Burgess (CPDT-KA)</a> who has over 20 years of experience in veterinary medicine and dog training.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading">In the Spotlight: Caring for Senior Dogs</h2>



<p>At Senior Tail Waggers, we specialize in senior dog care! More dogs are reaching &#8216;senior-citizen&#8217; status every year. This is down to ongoing advances in veterinary care and pet nutrition, plus the love and money we lavish on them. This is great news for them, and for us, because it means we get to enjoy more years with our furry best friend. But age can also bring a whole slew of changes and challenges for everyone.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>How can I make my old dog more comfortable?</strong></h2>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img decoding="async" width="1000" height="683" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;1000&#039;%20height=&#039;683&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%201000%20683&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="woman hugs senior dog" class="wp-image-6145 perfmatters-lazy" data-src="https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/woman-hug-senior-dog.jpg" data-srcset="https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/woman-hug-senior-dog.jpg 1000w, https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/woman-hug-senior-dog-300x205.jpg 300w, https://seniortailwaggers.com/wp-content/uploads/woman-hug-senior-dog-768x525.jpg 768w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px" /></figure>



<p>Diet, medication and simple changes in the household environment can have a massive impact on how dramatically your dog feels the effects of getting older. The earlier these changes are implemented, the more comfortable your dog’s transition into retirement will be:</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>1. Old dog proof your house</strong></h3>



<p><a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/treating-arthritis-in-senior-dogs/">Arthritis and mobility issues</a> are among the most common complaints owners have as their dog gets older. Stiffness first thing in the morning, muscle weakness and a reluctance to jump are just a few of the symptoms of aging joints. The household furnishings that once served as a playground for your younger dog may now seem more like an unnecessary obstacle course. Consider moving your dog’s bed and feeding bowl close together to limit the distance they need to travel for the essentials, and you might even want to block off the stairs to deter them from overexerting themselves. </p>



<p>The goal is to reduce the risk of accidents and increase comfort levels while still allowing your dog to maintain independence. </p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Comfy beds and elevated feeding bowls, are some of the essentials here. </li>



<li>Dog ramps are fantastic for helping them get in and out of the boot of the car, </li>



<li>Steps to get to their favorite spot on the couch, and </li>



<li>Grip pads on slippery surfaces can all hugely improve their quality of life.</li>
</ul>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>2. Watch for hot and cold temperatures</strong></h3>



<p>As dogs age, their metabolism slows down and generally isn’t as quick to respond to changes in their external environment as it once was. They are much more prone to feel the effects of extreme heat and cold so be sure to take extra precautions to keep them within their optimal temperature range. Protect against heat stroke by always taking plenty of water, icepacks and don’t stay out in the sun for too long with your elderly dog. Similarly, hypothermia is a threat in low-temperature conditions so it would be wise to provide a doggy jacket in areas of colder climates.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>3. Moderate exercise for old dogs</strong></h3>



<p>Your elderly dog may not be as athletic as they once were; heart and lung functions deteriorate over time and while it’s important for your dog to stay active, you must be aware not to overdo it. Rather than long periods of exercise, the senior dog will prefer shorter periods of moderate exercise more frequently. What does ‘moderate’ exercise actually mean?&nbsp; No matter what ‘issues’ he has, there are <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/exercising-older-dogs/"><strong>exercise options and games</strong></a> that your senior dog will be able to enjoy.</p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>4. Keep your senior dog entertained</strong></h3>



<p>Senior dogs also want to have fun. View our selection of the best <a href="https://seniortailwaggers.com/senior-dog-toys/">senior dog toys</a>.</p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Learn More About Caring For a Senior Dog</h2>
